            // Delay all analytics loading for better LCP
            if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
              // Load Ahrefs analytics after interaction
              let ahrefsLoaded = false;
              const loadAhrefs = function() {
                if (!ahrefsLoaded) {
                  ahrefsLoaded = true;
                  const ahrefsScript = document.createElement('script');
                  ahrefsScript.src = 'https://analytics.ahrefs.com/analytics.js';
                  ahrefsScript.setAttribute('data-key', '5WxpE9x9XgCk27FIUEerOw');
                  ahrefsScript.async = true;
                  document.head.appendChild(ahrefsScript);
                }
              };

              // CRITICAL: Defer Google Tag Manager until user interaction
              // This saves 195 KiB of unused JavaScript on initial load
              let gtmLoaded = false;

              // Bot detection - don't track bots in Google Analytics
              const isBot = function() {
                const botPatterns = [
                  /bot/i, /crawl/i, /spider/i, /slurp/i, /mediapartners/i,
                  /googlebot/i, /bingbot/i, /yandex/i, /baidu/i, /duckduck/i,
                  /facebookexternalhit/i, /twitterbot/i, /linkedinbot/i,
                  /whatsapp/i, /telegrambot/i, /pinterest/i, /applebot/i,
                  /semrush/i, /ahrefs/i, /moz/i, /screaming/i, /lighthouse/i,
                  /chrome-lighthouse/i, /pagespeed/i, /gtmetrix/i, /pingdom/i,
                  /uptimerobot/i, /statuscake/i, /headless/i, /phantom/i,
                  /selenium/i, /puppeteer/i, /playwright/i
                ];
                const ua = navigator.userAgent || '';
                return botPatterns.some(pattern => pattern.test(ua));
              };

              const loadGoogleAnalytics = function() {
                if (gtmLoaded) return;

                // Skip GA for bots - they inflate US traffic numbers
                if (isBot()) {
                  console.log('[GA] Bot detected, skipping analytics');
                  return;
                }

                gtmLoaded = true;

                const gtagScript = document.createElement('script');
                gtagScript.async = true;
                gtagScript.src = 'https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtag/js?id=G-DP6Z7PE6WX';
                document.head.appendChild(gtagScript);

                window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
                function gtag(){dataLayer.push(arguments);}
                window.gtag = gtag;

                gtagScript.onload = function() {
                  gtag('js', new Date());
                  gtag('config', 'G-DP6Z7PE6WX', {
                    page_title: document.title,
                    page_location: window.location.href,
                    send_page_view: true,
                    anonymize_ip: true,
                    allow_ad_personalization_signals: false,
                  });

                  // Track page performance metrics (non-blocking)
                  if (typeof performance !== 'undefined') {
                    requestIdleCallback(() => {
                      gtag('event', 'timing_complete', {
                        name: 'load',
                        value: Math.round(performance.now())
                      });

                      // Track LCP when available
                      if ('PerformanceObserver' in window) {
                        new PerformanceObserver((entryList) => {
                          const entries = entryList.getEntries();
                          const lastEntry = entries[entries.length - 1];
                          gtag('event', 'web_vitals', {
                            name: 'LCP',
                            value: Math.round(lastEntry.startTime),
                            event_category: 'performance'
                          });
                        }).observe({entryTypes: ['largest-contentful-paint']});
                      }
                    });
                  }

                  // Track user engagement with minimal performance impact
                  let engaged = false;
                  const trackEngagement = () => {
                    if (!engaged) {
                      engaged = true;
                      gtag('event', 'engaged_session', {
                        engagement_time_msec: Math.round(performance.now())
                      });
                    }
                  };

                  // Delayed engagement tracking (non-blocking)
                  requestIdleCallback(() => {
                    ['scroll', 'click', 'keydown', 'touchstart'].forEach(event =>
                      document.addEventListener(event, trackEngagement, { once: true, passive: true })
                    );
                  });

                  // Track article reads (for content analysis)
                  if (window.location.pathname.includes('/actualites/')) {
                    requestIdleCallback(() => {
                      gtag('event', 'page_view', {
                        page_title: document.title,
                        page_location: window.location.href,
                        content_group1: 'article'
                      });
                    });
                  }
                };
              };

              // Non-critical CSS removed to improve LCP performance

              // CRITICAL: Load analytics ONLY after user interaction (scroll, click, touch)
              // This saves 195 KiB on initial page load
              let analyticsInitialized = false;
              const initAnalytics = function() {
                if (analyticsInitialized) return;
                analyticsInitialized = true;

                // Load Ahrefs immediately on interaction
                loadAhrefs();

                // Load GTM with small delay after interaction
                setTimeout(loadGoogleAnalytics, 500);
              };

              // Listen for first user interaction
              const events = ['scroll', 'click', 'touchstart', 'keydown', 'mousemove'];
              events.forEach(event => {
                window.addEventListener(event, initAnalytics, { once: true, passive: true });
              });

              // Fallback: load after 10 seconds if no interaction
              setTimeout(initAnalytics, 10000);

              // Register Service Worker for caching third-party scripts
              // This fixes PageSpeed warning about poor cache headers (4 KiB savings)
              if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
                window.addEventListener('load', function() {
                  navigator.serviceWorker.register('/sw.js')
                    .then(function(registration) {
                      console.log('[ServiceWorker] Registered successfully:', registration.scope);
                    })
                    .catch(function(error) {
                      console.log('[ServiceWorker] Registration failed:', error);
                    });
                });
              }
            }
